# Policy Form Provisions

### Policy form clauses

+----------------------------------------------------------------------------------+ +----------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| WC 04 03 06 01 15 - CONDITION                                                    | | WC 00 00 01 A 01 15 - LIMITATION                                                 |

Applies within CT class 8810, Location 2; location ; class 8810; limit ; deductible . Annual Payroll: $686,739; Classification: Clerical office employees; Estimated Premium: $19,640; Form Title: Voluntary Compensation Endorsement; State: CT

***

WC 00 00 01 A 04 21 - CONDITION

**State Classification Control**

The CT classification 8810 controls the rating basis for Clerical office employees unless a state amendatory endorsement changes it.

Applies within CT class 8810, Location 2; location ; class 8810; limit ; deductible . Annual Payroll: $686,739; Classification: Clerical office employees; Estimated Premium: $19,640; Form Title: Voluntary Compensation Endorsement; State: CT

***

WC 00 00 01 A 04 21 - LIMITATION

**Officer And Subcontractor Treatment**

Officer, member, volunteer, leased-worker, and subcontractor treatment for CT class 8810, Location 2 must be read with the attached forms schedule.

Applies within CT class 8810, Location 2; location ; class 8810; limit ; deductible . Annual Payroll: $686,739; Classification: Clerical office employees; Estimated Premium: $19,640; Form Title: Voluntary Compensation Endorsement; State: CT

***

WC 00 00 01 A 04 21 - CONDITION

**Premium Revision Basis**

The estimated premium of $19,640 is calculated from rate 2.86, experience modification 1.04, and schedule rating 0%.

Applies within CT class 8810, Location 2; location ; class 8810; limit ; deductible . Annual Payroll: $686,739; Classification: Clerical office employees; Estimated Premium: $19,640; Form Title: Voluntary Compensation Endorsement; State: CT
